<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
	var initial_prop_type = 1;
	displayFiltersByPropertyType(initial_prop_type);
});
function clearPropSubTypes(){
	var sub_prop_types = document.getElementsByClassName("sub_prop_types");
	for (var i = 0; i < sub_prop_types.length; i++) {
		sub_prop_types[i].checked = false;
	}
}
function clearDistricts(){
	var districts = document.getElementsByClassName("districts");
	for (var i = 0; i < districts.length; i++) {
		districts[i].checked = false;
	}
}

function displayFilters(prop_type_element_id){
	var property_type = document.getElementById(prop_type_element_id).value;
	displayFiltersByPropertyType(property_type);
}

function displayFiltersByPropertyType(property_type){
	var hide_on_land = document.getElementsByClassName("hide_on_land");
	if(property_type == 2){
		for (var i = 0; i < hide_on_land.length; i++) {
			hide_on_land[i].style.display = "none";
		}
		var hide_on_land_check = document.getElementsByClassName("hide_on_land_check");
		for (var i = 0; i < hide_on_land_check.length; i++) {
			hide_on_land_check[i].checked = false;
		}
	}else{
		for (var i = 0; i < hide_on_land.length; i++) {
			hide_on_land[i].style.display = hide_on_land[i].dataset.showflex == "1" ? "flex" : "block";
		}
	}

	var show_on_land = document.getElementsByClassName("show_on_land");
	if(property_type == 2){
		for (var i = 0; i < show_on_land.length; i++) {
			show_on_land[i].style.display = "flex";
		}
	}else{
		for (var i = 0; i < show_on_land.length; i++) {
			show_on_land[i].style.display = "none";
		}
		var show_on_land_check = document.getElementsByClassName("show_on_land_check");
		for (var i = 0; i < show_on_land_check.length; i++) {
			show_on_land_check[i].checked = false;
		}
	}

	// PROPERTY_SPECS
	var propspecs_elements = document.getElementsByClassName('propspecs');
	for (var i = 0; i < propspecs_elements.length; i++) {
		var elem = propspecs_elements[i];
		var proptype = elem.dataset.proptype;
		var specid = elem.dataset.specid;

		if(proptype.includes(property_type)){
			$('.'+specid).show();
		}else{
			$('.'+specid).hide();
			elem.checked = false;
		}
	}
}
function changeCurrency(id){
	let currencyPicker = document.getElementById(id);
	let value = currencyPicker?.value || '';
	let minPriceInput = document.querySelector('input[name="min_price"]');
	let maxPriceInput = document.querySelector('input[name="max_price"]');

	let icon = '';
	switch (value){
		case '4': icon = '$'; break;
		case '2': icon = '₺'; break;
		case '1': icon = '£'; break;
		case '3': icon = '€'; break;
	}

	document.getElementById('min_currency_icon').innerHTML=icon;
	document.getElementById('max_currency_icon').innerHTML=icon;

	if (minPriceInput) {
		minPriceInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
			// Only set to GBP if no currency is currently selected
			if (currencyPicker.value === '' && this.value) {
				currencyPicker.value = '1'; // Set to GBP
				document.getElementById('min_currency_icon').innerHTML = '£';
				document.getElementById('max_currency_icon').innerHTML = '£';
			}
		});
	}

	if (maxPriceInput) {
		maxPriceInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
			// Only set to GBP if no currency is currently selected
			if (currencyPicker.value === '' && this.value) {
				currencyPicker.value = '1'; // Set to GBP
				document.getElementById('min_currency_icon').innerHTML = '£';
				document.getElementById('max_currency_icon').innerHTML = '£';
			}
		});
	}
}

// Initialize currency section on page load
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
	var currencyPicker = document.getElementById('currency_picker');
	if (currencyPicker) {
		changeCurrency('currency_picker');
	}
});
</script>

<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
function observedropdown(id) {
	var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
		mutations.forEach(function(mutationRecord) {
			checkdropdowns();
		});    
	});

	var target = document.getElementById(id);
	observer.observe(target, { attributes : true, attributeFilter : ['style'] });
}

function checkdropdowns() {
	let konut = document.getElementById('konut-tipi-dropdown').style['z-index'];
	let location = document.getElementById('location-dropdown').style['z-index'];
	let price = document.getElementById('price-dropdown').style['z-index'];
	let area = document.getElementById('area-dropdown').style['z-index'];
	let detail = document.getElementById('detail-dropdown').style['z-index'];

	let overlay = document.getElementById('dark-overlay');

	if (konut > 900 || location > 900 || price > 900 || area > 900 || detail > 900) {
		toggleScroll(false);
		overlay.style.display = "block";
	} else {
		toggleScroll(true);
		overlay.style.display = "none";
	}

}
</script>

<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
(function() {
    // Add onchange event to currency picker
    function initializeCurrencyPicker() {
        try {
            var currencyPicker = document.getElementById('currency_picker_mobile_sale');
            if (currencyPicker) {
                currencyPicker.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    changeCurrencyMobile('currency_picker_mobile_sale');
                });
                // Initialize on page load
                changeCurrencyMobile('currency_picker_mobile_sale');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error initializing currency picker:', error);
        }
    }

    function changeCurrencyMobile(id) {
        try {
            let currencyPicker = document.getElementById(id);
            let value = currencyPicker?.value || '';
            let minPriceInput = document.getElementById('min_price_mobile_sale');
            let maxPriceInput = document.getElementById('max_price_mobile_sale');

            if (minPriceInput) {
                minPriceInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                    // Only set to GBP if no currency is currently selected
                    if (currencyPicker.value === '' && this.value) {
                        currencyPicker.value = '1'; // Set to GBP
                    } 
                });
            }

            if (maxPriceInput) {
                maxPriceInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                    // Only set to GBP if no currency is currently selected
                    if (currencyPicker.value === '' && this.value) {
                        currencyPicker.value = '1'; // Set to GBP
                    }
                });
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error changing currency:', error);
        }
    }

    // Ensure the DOM is fully loaded before initializing
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeCurrencyPicker);
    } else {
        initializeCurrencyPicker();
    }
})();
</script>
				</form>
            </div>

<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
(function() {
    // Add onchange event to currency picker
    function initializeCurrencyPicker() {
        try {
            var currencyPicker = document.getElementById('currency_picker_mobile_rent');
            if (currencyPicker) {
                currencyPicker.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    changeCurrencyMobile('currency_picker_mobile_rent');
                });
                // Initialize on page load
                changeCurrencyMobile('currency_picker_mobile_rent');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error initializing currency picker:', error);
        }
    }

    function changeCurrencyMobile(id) {
        try {
            let currencyPicker = document.getElementById(id);
            let value = currencyPicker?.value || '';
            let minPriceInput = document.getElementById('min_price_mobile_rent');
            let maxPriceInput = document.getElementById('max_price_mobile_rent');

            if (minPriceInput) {
                minPriceInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                    // Only set to GBP if no currency is currently selected
                    if (currencyPicker.value === '' && this.value) {
                        currencyPicker.value = '1'; // Set to GBP
                    } 
                });
            }

            if (maxPriceInput) {
                maxPriceInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                    // Only set to GBP if no currency is currently selected
                    if (currencyPicker.value === '' && this.value) {
                        currencyPicker.value = '1'; // Set to GBP
                    }
                });
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error changing currency:', error);
        }
    }

    // Ensure the DOM is fully loaded before initializing
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeCurrencyPicker);
    } else {
        initializeCurrencyPicker();
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
(function() {
    // Add onchange event to currency picker
    function initializeCurrencyPicker() {
        try {
            var currencyPicker = document.getElementById('currency_picker_mobile_daily');
            if (currencyPicker) {
                currencyPicker.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    changeCurrencyMobile('currency_picker_mobile_daily');
                });
                // Initialize on page load
                changeCurrencyMobile('currency_picker_mobile_daily');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error initializing currency picker:', error);
        }
    }

    function changeCurrencyMobile(id) {
        try {
            let currencyPicker = document.getElementById(id);
            let value = currencyPicker?.value || '';
            let minPriceInput = document.getElementById('min_price_mobile_daily');
            let maxPriceInput = document.getElementById('max_price_mobile_daily');

            if (minPriceInput) {
                minPriceInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                    // Only set to GBP if no currency is currently selected
                    if (currencyPicker.value === '' && this.value) {
                        currencyPicker.value = '1'; // Set to GBP
                    } 
                });
            }

            if (maxPriceInput) {
                maxPriceInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                    // Only set to GBP if no currency is currently selected
                    if (currencyPicker.value === '' && this.value) {
                        currencyPicker.value = '1'; // Set to GBP
                    }
                });
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error changing currency:', error);
        }
    }

    // Ensure the DOM is fully loaded before initializing
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeCurrencyPicker);
    } else {
        initializeCurrencyPicker();
    }
})();
</script>

		<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
		
		function reloadRegisterPickers() {
			$('#register_cityTR').selectpicker('hide');
			$('#register_country').on('change',function(){
				var value = $(this).val();
				if(value == 270){
					$('#register_cityOTHER').hide();
					$('#register_cityTR').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityCY').selectpicker('show');
				}
				else if ( value == 1 ){
					$('#register_cityOTHER').hide();
					$('#register_cityCY').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityTR').selectpicker('show');
				}
				else if ( value > 1 ) {
					$('#register_cityCY').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityTR').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityOTHER').show();
				}
			});

			$('#register_cityTR_ind').selectpicker('hide');
			$('#register_country_ind').on('change',function(){
				var value = $(this).val();
				if(value == 270){
					$('#register_cityOTHER_ind').hide();
					$('#register_cityTR_ind').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityCY_ind').selectpicker('show');
				}
				else if ( value == 1 ){
					$('#register_cityOTHER_ind').hide();
					$('#register_cityCY_ind').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityTR_ind').selectpicker('show');
				}
				else if ( value > 1 ) {
					$('#register_cityCY_ind').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityTR_ind').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityOTHER_ind').show();
				}
			});

			$('#register_cityTR_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
			$('#register_country_mobile').on('change',function(){
				var value = $(this).val();
				if(value == 270){
					$('#register_cityOTHER_mobile').hide();
					$('#register_cityTR_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityCY_mobile').selectpicker('show');
				}
				else if ( value == 1 ){
					$('#register_cityOTHER_mobile').hide();
					$('#register_cityCY_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityTR_mobile').selectpicker('show');
				}
				else if ( value > 1 ) {
					$('#register_cityCY_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityTR_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityOTHER_mobile').show();
				}
			});

			$('#register_cityTR_ind_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
			$('#register_country_ind_mobile').on('change',function(){
				var value = $(this).val();
				if(value == 270){
					$('#register_cityOTHER_ind_mobile').hide();
					$('#register_cityTR_ind_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityCY_ind_mobile').selectpicker('show');
				}
				else if ( value == 1 ){
					$('#register_cityOTHER_ind_mobile').hide();
					$('#register_cityCY_ind_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityTR_ind_mobile').selectpicker('show');
				}
				else if ( value > 1 ) {
					$('#register_cityCY_ind_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityTR_ind_mobile').selectpicker('hide');
					$('#register_cityOTHER_ind_mobile').show();
				}
			});

			$('#register_user_type').on('change',function(){
				var value = $(this).val();
				if( value == 'M' ){
					$('#register_authorized').val('');
					$('#register_authorized_div').hide();
					
					$('#register_reason').show().prop('required',true);
				}else{
					$('#register_authorized_div').show();
					
					$('#register_reason').hide().prop('required',false);
				}
			});

		}
		reloadRegisterPickers();
	</script>

	<script src="/v4/vendors/intlTelInput/js/intlTelInput.js" type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript"></script>
	<script src="/v4/vendors/intlTelInput/js/utils.js" type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript"></script>
	<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">	
		document.querySelectorAll("input.intlPhone").forEach(function(element) {
			initialise(element);
		});

		function initialise(item)
		{
            var itemId = item.id;
            var itemName = item.name;

            if (!document.getElementById(itemId + 'CountryCode')) {
                var hiddenInput = document.createElement('input');
                hiddenInput.type = 'hidden';
                hiddenInput.id = itemId + 'CountryCode';
                hiddenInput.name = itemName + 'CountryCode';

                item.parentNode.insertBefore(hiddenInput, item.nextSibling);
            }
			//hata div'inin id'sini belirtir
			var errordiv = $(this).attr('id') + 'info';
			$('#' + errordiv).hide();
			var iti = window.intlTelInput(item, {
				initialCountry: "tr",
				showSelectedDialCode: false,
				i18n: { 'tr' : 'Türkiye' },
				autoInsertDialCode: true,
				utilsScript: "/v4/vendors/intlTelInput/js/utils.js",
				preferredCountries:['trnc', 'tr', 'gb', 'ru', 'de', 'fr', 'us'],
				countrySearch: false
			});
			if(item.value != ""){
				item.classList.remove("error");
				item.value = iti.getNumber();
				var countryCode = iti.getSelectedCountryData().dialCode;
				document.getElementById(itemId + 'CountryCode').value = '+' + countryCode;
			}
			item.addEventListener("countrychange", function() {
				var countryCode = iti.getSelectedCountryData().dialCode;
				document.getElementById(itemId + 'CountryCode').value = '+' + countryCode;
			});
			item.addEventListener('change', function() {

				if(!iti.isValidNumber() && item.value != ""){
					item.classList.add("error");
					item.value = "";
					$.notify({
						title: "<h3>Incorrect Phone</h3>",
						message: "You entered an incorrect phone number.", },{
						type: 'warning',
						placement: {
							from: "top",
							align: "center"
						},
						delay: 1000,
						timer: 5000
					});
				}
				else{
					item.classList.remove("error");
					item.value = iti.getNumber();
					var countryCode = iti.getSelectedCountryData().dialCode;
					document.getElementById(itemId + 'CountryCode').value = '+' + countryCode;
				}
			});
		}

		$('.add-favorite').on('click',function(){
			var a_obj = $(this);
			var propid = $(this).data('propid');
			var data = {
				propertyid: propid,
				notes: '',
				dowhat: 'addremove'
			};
			$.ajax({
				url: "/DML/property-detail/add-remove-favourites",
				type: "POST",
				data: data,
				success: function (data) {
					if(data == 'ADD' ){
						a_obj.children().attr("src","/v4/images/favourite_filled.svg");
						$.notify({
							title: "<h3>Favorites</h3>",
							message: "Ad has been added to your favorites", },{
							type: 'success',
							placement: {
								from: "top",
								align: "center"
							},
							delay: 5000
						});
					}else if( data == 'REMOVE' ){
						a_obj.children().attr("src","/v4/images/favourite.svg");

						$.notify({
							title: "<h3>Favorites</h3>",
							message: "Ad removed from favorites", },{
							type: 'warning',
							placement: {
								from: "top",
								align: "center"
							},
							delay: 5000
						});
					}
				},
				error: function (xhr, status, error) {
				
				}
			});                            
			});
		$('.add-compare').on('click',function(event){
			event.preventDefault();
			var a_obj = $(this);
			var propid = $(this).data('propid');
			var data = {
				id: propid,
				compare_list: 'property'
			};
			$.ajax({
				url: "/ac/add-to-compare",
				type: "POST",
				data: data,
				dataType: 'json',
				success: function (data) {
										if(data.result == 'added' ){
						if(a_obj.data('changeopacity')!=false){
							a_obj.parent().css('opacity','1');
						}
					}else if( data.result == 'list_full' ){
						$.notify({
							title: "<h3>Compare Ads</h3>",
							message: "You can compare up to 4 ads!", },{
							type: 'warning',
							placement: {
								from: "top",
								align: "center"
							},
							delay: 5000,
							timer: 400,
							animate: {
								enter: '',
								exit: ''
							}
						});
					//}else if ( data.result == 'duplicate' ){
					}else if ( data.result == 'removed' ) {
						if(a_obj.data('changeopacity')!=false){					
							a_obj.parent().css('opacity','0.5');
						}
					}
					$('#compare-count').html(data.count);
					if(data.count>0){ 
						$('.compareListButton').show();
					}else {
						$('.compareListButton').hide();
					}
				},
				error: function (xhr, status, error) {
				
				}
			});                            
		});
	</script>

	<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
		function regenerateCache(path, filterName, e){
			var data = {
				path: path,
				filter_name: filterName
			};
			$.ajax({
				url: "/ac/regenerate_filter",
				type: "POST",
				data: data,
				dataType: 'json',
				success: function (data) {
					if(data.result == 'ok'){
						e.src = e.src;
					}else{
						e.onerror=null;
						e.src="/v4/images/no-image.jpg";
					}
				},
				error: function (xhr, status, error) {
				}
			});
		}
	</script>
		<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
		var call_phone_ids = [];
		var send_whatsapp_ids = [];
		var show_phone_ids = [];

		function handleWhatsappClick(propertyid, userid, agentid) {
			if(send_whatsapp_ids.indexOf(propertyid) === -1) {
				send_whatsapp_ids.push(propertyid);
				addBtnClickEvent(propertyid, userid, agentid, 'send_whatsapp_listing');
			}
		}
		function handleCallPhoneClick(propertyid, userid, agentid) {
			if(call_phone_ids.indexOf(propertyid) === -1) {
				call_phone_ids.push(propertyid);
				addBtnClickEvent(propertyid, userid, agentid, 'call_phone_listing');
			}
		}

		function handleShowPhoneClick(propertyid, userid, agentid) {
			if(show_phone_ids.indexOf(propertyid) === -1) {
				show_phone_ids.push(propertyid);
				addBtnClickEvent(propertyid, userid, agentid, 'show_phone_listing');
			}
		}
		
		function addBtnClickEvent(propertyid, userid, agentid, btntype){
			var params = "propertyid=" + propertyid + "&btntype=" + btntype + "&userid=" + userid + "&useragentid=" + agentid;
			var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
			request.open("POST", "/ac/button-click", true);
			request.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8');

			request.onreadystatechange = function() {
				if (this.readyState == XMLHttpRequest.DONE && this.status == 200) {
					var result = request.response;
					// console.log(result);
					// var result = JSON.parse(result);
				}
			};

			request.onerror = function() {
			};
			request.send(params);
		}
	</script>

	<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
		function redirect_to_route(proptype) {
var path;
path = 'start';

if (proptype == 1) {
path = '/north-cyprus/houses-for-sale';
} else if (proptype == 2) {
path = '/north-cyprus/lands-for-sale';
} else if (proptype == 3) {
path = '/north-cyprus/commercial-for-sale';
} else {
path = '/north-cyprus/property-for-sale';
} path = path.replace(/&amp;/g, '&')
window.location.replace(path);
}

	<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function (event) {
var url = "/ac/search-result";
var params = "s_r=S&property_type=1&city=famagusta";
var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
request.open('POST', url, true);
request.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8');

request.onreadystatechange = function () {
if (this.readyState == XMLHttpRequest.DONE && this.status == 200) {
var count = request.responseText;
var page_number = ((count < 30) ? 1 : Math.ceil(count / 30));
var page_index = "1";
document.getElementById('page_number').innerHTML = page_number;
document.getElementById('count_label').innerHTML = thousandSeparator(request.responseText) + " Results Found";
var x = document.getElementById("pagination_select");
var i;
for (i = 2; i <= page_number; i++) {
  var option = document.createElement("option");
  var path = "/north-cyprus/houses-for-sale/famagusta?s_r=S&property_type=1&page=varx&sort=mr";
  option.text = i;
  option.value=path.replace("page=varx", "page="+i);
  if (page_index == i){
      option.selected = true;
  }
  x.add(option);
}
if (page_index == 1) {
document.getElementById("pagination_previous").classList.add("disabled-link");
document.getElementById("pagination_previous").removeAttribute("href");
}
if (page_number == page_index) {
document.getElementById("pagination_next").classList.add("disabled-link");
document.getElementById("pagination_next").removeAttribute("href");
}
$('#pagination_select').selectpicker('refresh');
} else {}
};

request.onerror = function () {};

request.send(params);
});

$('.currency_select').on('change', function () {
$('.currency_symbol').html('₺');
});
	</script>

<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
function showphone(id, phone, user_id, user_agent_id) {
	var nullable_user_agent_id = user_agent_id ? user_agent_id : '';
	var clicked_element_id = "listing-call-phone-#"+user_id+"#"+nullable_user_agent_id+"#"+id;
	var clicked_element = document.getElementById(clicked_element_id);
	if(clicked_element) {
		
		if(clicked_element.dataset.label == "show"){
			//set clicked element data-label to "show"
			clicked_element.href = "tel:"+phone;
			handleCallPhoneClick(id, user_id, user_agent_id);
		} else {
			let eid = "a-" + id;
			let element = document.getElementById(eid);
			element.innerHTML = phone;
			clicked_element.setAttribute("data-label", "show");
			handleShowPhoneClick(id, user_id, user_agent_id);
		}
	}
	//let eid = `listing-call-phone-#${user_id}#${user_agent_id ? user_agent_id : ''}#${id}`;
	

}
</script>

function toggleScroll(enable) {
	if (enable) {
		document.querySelector('body').classList.remove('no-scroll');
	} else {
		document.querySelector('body').classList.add('no-scroll');
	}
}

<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
function replacesubmit(type, form_id) {
	document.getElementById('s-r').value= type;
	document.getElementById('mobile-submit').setAttribute('onclick', `javascript:document.getElementById('${form_id}').submit()`);
}
function thousandSeparator(n, sep) {
	var sRegExp = new RegExp('(-?[0-9]+)([0-9]{3})');
	var sValue = n + '';
	if (sep === undefined) {
		sep = '.';
	}
	while (sRegExp.test(sValue)) {
		sValue = sValue.replace(sRegExp, '$1' + sep + '$2');
	}
	return sValue;
}

function mobileFilterIlanItemClick() {
	$('#district_sale_mobile').selectpicker('refresh');
	$('#district_rent_mobile').selectpicker('refresh');
	$('#district_daily_mobile').selectpicker('refresh');
}

$( document ).ready(function() {
    mobileFilterIlanItemClick();
});

	<script type="d0eafbfc4be2f30f90955582-text/javascript">
		function toggleScroll(enable) {
			if (enable) {
				document.querySelector('body').classList.remove('no-scroll');
			} else {
				document.querySelector('body').classList.add('no-scroll');
			}
		}

		$(function () {
			$('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip()
		})

		 
		function formatNumber(num) {
			return num.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ",");
		}

		function unformatNumber(num) {
			return num.replace(/,/g, '');
		}

		document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
			const priceInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="min_price"], input[name="max_price"]');

			priceInputs.forEach(function(input) {
				
				input.addEventListener('input', function(event) {
					const cursorPos = this.selectionStart;
					
					let rawValue = this.value.replace(/\D/g, '');
					
					if (rawValue) {
						const formattedValue = formatNumber(rawValue);
						
						if (this.value !== formattedValue) {
							this.value = formattedValue;
							
							const addedCommas = formattedValue.length - rawValue.length;
							this.setSelectionRange(cursorPos + addedCommas, cursorPos + addedCommas);
						}
					}
				});

				input.closest('form')?.addEventListener('submit', function(event) {
					priceInputs.forEach(input => {
						input.value = unformatNumber(input.value);
					});
				});
			});
			
			const areaInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="min_m2"], input[name="max_m2"]');

			areaInputs.forEach(function(input) {
				input.addEventListener('input', function(event) {
					this.value = this.value.replace(/\D/g, '');
				});
			});
		});

		$(document).on('tap','.w-inline-block.w-lightbox', function(){
			$('div.w-lightbox-content.w-lightbox-group').off('swipe');    
		});
	</script>
